      "description": "Create the .p8 parser \u2014 shared foundation for all test layers",
      "file_text": "\"\"\"\np8_parser.py \u2014 Parse a PICO-8 .p8 cartridge into structured data.\n\nExtracts:\n- Lua source code\n- String-packed data tables (_j, _s, _r, _e)\n- Sprite pixel data from __gfx__\n- Sprite flags from __gff__\n- Section raw text\n\"\"\"\nimport re\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any\n\n\ndef parse_p8(filepath: str) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Parse a .p8 file into a structured dict.\"\"\"\n    with open(filepath, \"r\") as f:\n        content = f.read()\n\n    sections = extract_sections(content)\n    lua = sections.get(\"lua\", \"\")\n\n    return {\n        \"sections\": sections,\n        \"lua\": lua,\n        \"data\": extract_data_tables(lua),\n        \"sprites\": parse_gfx(sections.get(\"gfx\", \"\")),\n        \"flags\": parse_gff(sections.get(\"gff\", \"\")),\n        \"functions\": extract_functions(lua),\n        \"source_lines\": lua.split(\"\\n\"),\n    }\n\n\ndef extract_sections(content: str) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Split .p8 content into named sections.\"\"\"\n    sections = {}\n    current = None\n    lines = content.split(\"\\n\")\n    buf = []\n\n    for line in lines:\n        m = re.match(r\"^__(\\w+)__$\", line)\n        if m:\n            if current:\n                sections[current] = \"\\n\".join(buf)\n            current = m.group(1)\n            buf = []\n        elif current:\n            buf.append(line)\n\n    if current:\n        sections[current] = \"\\n\".join(buf)\n\n    return sections\n\n\ndef extract_data_tables(lua: str) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Extract pipe-delimited string-packed data tables from Lua source.\n\n    Finds patterns like: _j=pd(\"...|...|...\")\n    Returns dict mapping variable name -> list of lists of strings.\n    \"\"\"\n    tables = {}\n    # Match _varname=pd(\"...\")\n    pattern = r'(_\\w+)\\s*=\\s*pd\\(\\s*\"([^\"]*)\"\\s*\\)'\n    for match in re.finditer(pattern, lua):\n        varname = match.group(1)\n        raw = match.group(2)\n        rows = []\n        for row_str in raw.split(\"|\"):\n            rows.append(row_str.split(\",\"))\n        tables[varname] = rows\n\n    # Also extract simple split tables like: jn=split(\"squire,knight,...\")\n    pattern2 = r'(\\w+)\\s*=\\s*split\\(\\s*\"([^\"]*)\"\\s*\\)'\n    for match in re.finditer(pattern2, lua):\n        varname = match.group(1)\n        raw = match.group(2)\n        tables[varname] = raw.split(\",\")\n\n    return tables\n\n\ndef parse_gfx(gfx_text: str) -> Dict[int, List[List[int]]]:\n    \"\"\"Parse __gfx__ hex data into per-sprite pixel arrays.\n\n    Returns dict: sprite_index -> 8x8 list of color values (0-15).\n    \"\"\"\n    sprites = {}\n    lines = [l for l in gfx_text.strip().split(\"\\n\") if l]\n\n    if len(lines) != 128:\n        return sprites\n\n    for sprite_row in range(16):\n        for sprite_col in range(16):\n            sprite_idx = sprite_row * 16 + sprite_col\n            pixels = []\n            for pixel_row in range(8):\n                line_idx = sprite_row * 8 + pixel_row\n                if line_idx >= len(lines):\n                    pixels.append([0] * 8)\n                    continue\n                line = lines[line_idx]\n                start = sprite_col * 8\n                end = start + 8\n                if end <= len(line):\n                    row_hex = line[start:end]\n                    pixels.append([int(c, 16) for c in row_hex])\n                else:\n                    pixels.append([0] * 8)\n            sprites[sprite_idx] = pixels\n\n    return sprites\n\n\ndef parse_gff(gff_text: str) -> Dict[int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Parse __gff__ sprite flags.\n\n    Returns dict: sprite_index -> flags byte (0-255).\n    \"\"\"\n    flags = {}\n    lines = [l for l in gff_text.strip().split(\"\\n\") if l]\n\n    for line_idx, line in enumerate(lines[:2]):\n        for i in range(0, min(len(line), 256), 2):\n            sprite_idx = line_idx * 128 + i // 2\n            flags[sprite_idx] = int(line[i : i + 2], 16)\n\n    return flags\n\n\ndef extract_functions(lua: str) -> Dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract function bodies from Lua source.\n\n    Returns dict: function_name -> full function source including body.\n    Simple heuristic: match 'function name(' and count end keywords.\n    \"\"\"\n    functions = {}\n    lines = lua.split(\"\\n\")\n    i = 0\n    while i < len(lines):\n        m = re.match(r\"^\\s*function\\s+(\\w+)\\s*\\(\", lines[i])\n        if m:\n            fname = m.group(1)\n            depth = 1\n            start = i\n            i += 1\n            while i < len(lines) and depth > 0:\n                line = lines[i].strip()\n                # Count depth changes (simplified)\n                # Openers: function, if...then, for...do, while...do, repeat\n                if re.match(\n                    r\"^(function\\b|if\\b.*\\bthen\\b|for\\b.*\\bdo\\b|while\\b.*\\bdo\\b|repeat\\b)\",\n                    line,\n                ):\n                    # But single-line if (no matching end) \u2014 check if end is on same line\n                    if not (line.startswith(\"if\") and \"end\" in line and \"then\" in line):\n                        # Check for single-line if: if (cond) stmt\n                        if not re.match(r\"^if\\s*\\(.*\\)\\s+\\S\", line):\n                            depth += 1\n                if re.match(r\"^end\\b\", line):\n                    depth -= 1\n                i += 1\n            functions[fname] = \"\\n\".join(lines[start:i])\n        else:\n            i += 1\n\n    return functions\n\n\ndef sprite_has_pixels(sprite_pixels: List[List[int]]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a sprite has any non-zero (non-black) pixels.\"\"\"\n    for row in sprite_pixels:\n        for pixel in row:\n            if pixel != 0:\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef get_job(data: dict, job_id: int) -> Optional[dict]:\n    \"\"\"Get a job by 1-indexed ID from parsed b.x) + abs(a.y - b.y)\\n\\n    def calc_damage(self, attacker, defender, power=0):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Damage formula matching Lua: max(1, power + atk + relic - def)\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        atk_bonus = self.relic_bonus(\\\"atk\\\", attacker.team)\\n        return max(1, power + attacker.atk + atk_bonus - 1) Try heal if anyone is low\\n        for i, sk in enumerate(skills):\\n            sk_key = sk[\\\"name\\\"]\\n            if sk[\\\"type\\\"] == \\\"h\\\" and unit.cooldowns.get(sk_key, 0) == 0:\\n                target = None\\n                for f in friends:\\n                    if f.hp < f.max_hp * 0.5:\\n                        if target is None or f.hp < target.hp:\\n                            target = f\\n                if target:\\n                    power = sk[\\\"power\\\"] + self.relic_bonus(\\\"atk\\\", unit.team)\\n                    target.hp = min(target.max_hp, target.hp + power)\\n                    unit.cooldowns[sk_key] = sk[\\\"cd\\\"]\\n                    self.log.append(f\\\"{unit.name} heals {target.name} for {power}\\\")\\n                    return\\n\\n        # 2) Find target (behavior-aware, matches Lua doact)\\n        nearest = None\\n        nearest_dist = 999\\n        bf = unit.behavior\\n\\n        for f in foes:\\n            d = self.manhattan(unit, f)\\n            if bf == 1:\\n                # Target lowest HP (assassin/focus fire)\\n                if (nearest is None or f.hp < nearest.hp\\n                        or (f.hp == nearest.hp and d < nearest_dist)):\\n                    nearest = f\\n                    nearest_dist = d\\n            elif bf == 2:\\n                # Target furthest back (lowest x = backrow)\\n                if (nearest is None or f.x < nearest.x\\n                        or (f.x == nearest.x and d < nearest_dist)):\\n                    nearest = f\\n                    nearest_dist = d\\n            else:\\n                # knight back\n            sim.make_player_unit(3, x=4, y=1),   # mage front\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),   # priest back\n        ]\n        enemies = [\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\n            sim.make_enemy(3, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\n        ]\n        return party, enemies\n\n    back_res = run_batch(cart, back_setup, N, seed_base=1000)\n    front_res = run_batch(cart, front_setup, N, seed_base=2000)\n    back_wr = win_rate(back_res)\n    front_wr = win_rate(front_res)\n    back_mage_surv = sum(1 for r in back_res if r.won and r.party[1].alive) / max(1, sum(1 for r in back_res if r.won))\n    front_mage_surv = sum(1 for r in front_res if r.won and r.party[1].alive) / max(1, sum(1 for r in front_res if r.won))\n    results[\"D1_back_wr\"] = back_wr\n    results[\"D1_front_wr\"] = front_wr\n    results[\"D1_mage_surv_diff\"] = back_mage_surv - front_mage_surv\n    print(f\"D1 Positioning: back WR {back_wr:.1%}, front WR {front_wr:.1%}, mage surv diff {back_mage_surv - front_mage_surv:.1%}\")\n    print(f\"   PASS\" if back_mage_surv - front_mage_surv > 0.10 else f\"   FAIL (need >10% diff)\")\n\n    # D4: Speed balance\\n    def fast_vs_slow(sim, i):\\n        party = [\\n            sim.make_player_unit(3, x=0, y=0),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(3, x=1, y=1),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),\\n        ]\\n        enemies = [\\n            sim.make_enemy(4, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(4, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(4, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\\n        ]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    spd_res = run_batch(cart, fast_vs_slow, N, seed_base=7000)\\n    spd_wr = win_rate(spd_res)\\n    results[\\\"D4_speed_wr\\\"] = spd_wr\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nD4 Speed: fast(spd4) vs slow(spd2) ogres: {spd_wr:.1%}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"   PASS\\\" if spd_wr < 0.95 else f\\\"   FAIL (need <95%)\\\")\\n\\n    # D5: Relic differentiation\\n    for stat, label in [(\\\"a\\\", \\\"ATK\\\"), (\\\"d\\\", \\\"DEF\\\")]:\\n        relics = [r for r in cart.relics if r[\\\"stat_key\\\"] == stat]\\n        if relics:\\n            rstack = (relics * 3)[:3]\\n            def rel_setup(sim, i, rs=rstack):\\n                sim.relics = rs\\n                party = [\\n                    sim.make_player_unit(1, x=0, y=0),\\n                    sim.make_player_unit(2, x=1, y=1),\\n                    sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),\\n                ]\\n                enemies = [\\n                    sim.make_enemy(3, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\\n                    sim.make_enemy(4, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\\n                    sim.make_enemy(3, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\\n                ]\\n                return party, enemies\\n            res = run_batch(cart, rel_setup, N, seed_base=8000 if stat==\\\"a\\\" else 8500)\\n            wr = win_rate(res)\\n            results[f\\\"D5_{label}_wr\\\"] = wr\\n            print(f\\\"\\\\nD5 Relics ({label} x3): WR {wr:.1%}\\\")\\n    diff = abs(results.get(\\\"D5_ATK_wr\\\", 0) - results.get(\\\"D5_DEF_wr\\\", 0))\\n    print(f\\\"   Diff: {diff:.1%}, PASS\\\" if diff > 0.05 else f\\\"   Diff: {diff:.1%}, FAIL (need >5%)\\\")\\n\\n    # D6: Wolf matchup\\n    def slow_wolf(sim, i):\\n        party = [sim.make_player_unit(2, x=0, y=j) for j in range(3)]\\n        enemies = [sim.make_enemy(3, x=5, y=j, floor=2) for j in range(3)]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    def fast_wolf(sim, i):\\n        party = [sim.make_player_unit(3, x=0, y=j) for j in range(3)]\\n        enemies = [sim.make_enemy(3, x=5, y=j, floor=2) for j in range(3)]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    slow_res = run_batch(cart, slow_wolf, N, seed_base=9000)\\n    fast_res = run_batch(cart, fast_wolf, N, seed_base=9500)\\n    results[\\\"D6_slow_wr\\\"] = win_rate(slow_res)\\n    results[\\\"D6_fast_wr\\\"] = win_rate(fast_res)\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nD6 Wolves: slow team {win_rate(slow_res):.1%}, fast team {win_rate(fast_res):.1%}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"   PASS\\\" if win_rate(fast_res) > win_rate(slow_res) + 0.05 else \\\"   FAIL\\\")\\n\\n    # D7: Campfire balance\\n    def healed(sim, i):\\n        party = [\\n            sim.make_player_unit(1, x=0, y=0),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(2, x=1, y=1),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),\\n        ]\\n        enemies = [\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(3, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\\n        ]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    def unhealed(sim, i):\\n        party = [\\n            sim.make_player_unit(1, x=0, y=0),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(2, x=1, y=1),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),\\n        ]\\n        for u in party:\\n            u.hp = max(1, int(u.max_hp * 0.4))\\n        enemies = [\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(3, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\\n        ]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    def upgraded(sim, i):\\n        party = [\\n            sim.make_player_unit(1, x=0, y=0),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(2, x=1, y=1),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2),\\n        ]\\n        for u in party:\\n            u.hp = max(1, int(u.max_hp * 0.4))\\n            u.atk += 1\\n        enemies = [\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=0, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(3, x=4, y=1, floor=2),\\n            sim.make_enemy(2, x=5, y=2, floor=2),\\n        ]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    h_res = run_batch(cart, healed, N, seed_base=10000)\\n    u_res = run_batch(cart, upgraded, N, seed_base=11000)\\n    results[\\\"D7_healed_wr\\\"] = win_rate(h_res)\\n    results[\\\"D7_upgraded_wr\\\"] = win_rate(u_res)\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nD7 Campfire: healed WR {win_rate(h_res):.1%}, upgraded (40%hp) WR {win_rate(u_res):.1%}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"   PASS\\\" if win_rate(h_res) > win_rate(u_res) else \\\"   FAIL\\\")\\n\\n    # D8: Boss balance\\n    def boss(sim, i):\\n        party = [\\n            sim.make_player_unit(2, x=0, y=0, level=3),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(3, x=0, y=1, level=3),\\n            sim.make_player_unit(4, x=0, y=2, level=3),\\n        ]\\n        enemies = [sim.make_enemy(5, x=5, y=1, floor=3)]\\n        return party, enemies\\n    boss_res = run_batch(cart, boss, N, seed_base=12000)\\n    bwr = win_rate(boss_res)\\n    results[\\\"D8_boss_wr\\\"] = bwr\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nD8 Boss: WR {bwr:.1%}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"   PASS\\\" if 0.30 <= bwr <= 0.90 else f\\\"   FAIL (need 30-90%)\\\")\\n\\n    # They cannot bypass.\n        Behavior 1 (assassin) and 2 (backline) can target anyone.\n        \"\"\"\n        bf = unit.behavior\n        if bf == 0 and unit.team == 2:\n            # Find frontmost column with alive foes\n            max_x = max(f.x for f in foes)\n            front = [f for f in foes if f.x == max_x]\n            if front:\n                return front\n        return foes\n\n    def do_action(self, unit, all_units):\n        \"\"\"Override do_action with front-row blocking.\"\"\"\n        friends = [u for u in all_units if u.alive and u.team == unit.team]\n        foes = [u for u in all_units if u.alive and u.team != unit.team]\n        if not foes:\n            return\n\n        skills = self.get_skills_for(unit)\n\n        # Decrement buff\n        if unit.buff_turns > 0:\n            unit.buff_turns -= 1\n            if unit.buff_turns <= 0:\n                unit.def_ -= unit.buff_def\n                unit.buff_def = 0\n\n        # 1) Try heal\n        for i, sk in enumerate(skills):\n            sk_key = sk[\"name\"]\n            if sk[\"type\"] == \"h\" and unit.cooldowns.get(sk_key, 0) == 0:\n                target = None\n                for f in friends:\n                    if f.hp < f.max_hp * 0.5:\n                        if target is None or f.hp < target.hp:\n                            target = f\n                if target:\n                    power = sk[\"power\"] + self.relic_bonus(\"atk\", unit.team)\n                    target.hp = min(target.max_hp, target.hp + power)\n                    unit.cooldowns[sk_key] = sk[\"cd\"]\n                    self.log.append(f\"{unit.name} heals {target.name} for {power}\")\n                    return\n\n        # 2) Find target with blocking\n        target_pool = self.get_target_pool(unit, foes)\n        nearest = None\n        nearest_dist = 999\n        bf = unit.behavior\n\n        for f in target_pool:\n            d = self.manhattan(unit, f)\n            if bf == 1:\n                if nearest is None or f.hp < nearest.hp or (f.hp == nearest.hp and d < nearest_dist):\n                    nearest = f\n                    nearest_dist = d\n            elif bf == 2:\n                if nearest is None or f.x < nearest.x or (f.x == nearest.x and d < nearest_dist):\n                    nearest = f\n                    nearest_dist = d\n            else:\n                if d < nearest_dist:\n                    nearest = f\n                    nearest_dist = d\n\n        if nearest:\n            nearest_dist = self.manhattan(unit, nearest)\n\n        # 3) Try buff/block\n        for i, sk in enumerate(skills):\n            sk_key = sk[\"name\"]\n            if sk[\"type\"] == \"b\" and unit.cooldowns.get(sk_key, 0) == 0:\n                if nearest_dist <= 2:\n                    if unit.buff_def > 0:\n                        unit.def_ -= unit.buff_def\n                    unit.buff_def = sk[\"power\"]\n                    unit.buff_turns = 2\n                    unit.def_ += unit.buff_def\n                    unit.cooldowns[sk_key] = sk[\"cd\"]\n                    self.log.append(f\"{unit.name} uses {sk['name']} (+{sk['power']} def)\")\n                    return\n\n        # 5) Move or basic attack\n        if nearest_dist > 1:\n            if nearest.x > unit.x: unit.x += 1\n            elif nearest.x < unit.x: unit.x -= 1\n            elif nearest.y > unit.y: unit.y += 1\n            elif nearest.y < unit.y: unit.y -= 1\n            self.log.append(f\"{unit.name} moves to ({unit.x},{unit.y})\")\n        else:\n            dmg = self.calc_damage(unit, nearest)\n            nearest.hp -= dmg\n            if nearest.hp <= 0:\n                nearest.alive = False\n            self.log.append(f\"{unit.name} attacks {nearest.name} for {dmg}\")\n\n\ndef run_tuned_batch(cart, setup_fn, n=500, seed_base=0):\n    \"\"\"Like run_batch but uses TunedCombatSim.\"\"\"\n    from tests.combat_sim import CombatResult\n    results = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        sim = TunedCombatSim(cart, rng_seed=seed_base + i)\n        party, enemies = setup_fn(sim, i)\n        result = sim.run(party, enemies)\n        results.append(result)\n    return results",
